       <script>
        function setCookieWidget() {
            try {
                var ddlDestinationClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlDestination';
                var ddlCityClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlCity';
                var ddlPropertyClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlProperty';
                var ddlRateTypeClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlRateType';
                var txtPromotionCodeClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_txtPromotionCode';
                var txtIATACodeClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_txtIATACode';
                var txtArrivalDateClientId = 'txtArrivalDate';
                var txtDepartureDateClientId = 'txtDepartureDate';

                var ddlRoomsClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_txtRoomNumber';
                var hdnIsSmokingProperty = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_hdnIsSmokingProperty';
                var hdnIsAccessibleProperty = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_hdnIsAccessibleRoom';
                var countryIndexValue = document.getElementById(ddlDestinationClientId).value;
                var destinationIndexValue = document.getElementById(ddlCityClientId).value;
                var propertyIndexValue = document.getElementById(ddlPropertyClientId).value;
                var rateTypeIndexValue = document.getElementById(ddlRateTypeClientId).value;
                var promoCodeValue = document.getElementById(txtPromotionCodeClientId).value;
                var iataCodeValue = document.getElementById(txtIATACodeClientId).value;

                var arrivalValue = document.getElementById(txtArrivalDateClientId).value;
                var departureValue = document.getElementById(txtDepartureDateClientId).value;
                var roomsValue = document.getElementById(ddlRoomsClientId).value;

                var isSmokingProperty = document.getElementById(hdnIsSmokingProperty).value;
                var isAccessibleProperty = document.getElementById(hdnIsAccessibleProperty).value;

                var value = countryIndexValue + '|' + destinationIndexValue + '|' + propertyIndexValue + '|' +
                            rateTypeIndexValue + '|' + promoCodeValue + '|' + iataCodeValue + '|' + arrivalValue
                            + '|' + departureValue + '|' + roomsValue + '|' + isSmokingProperty + '|' + isAccessibleProperty;
                setCookie("FairmontWidget", value, 1);


            }
            catch (ex) {
            }
        }

        function setCookie(c_name, value, exdays) {
            var exdate = new Date();
            exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
            var c_value = escape(value) + ((exdays == null) ? "" : "; expires=" + exdate.toUTCString());
            document.cookie = c_name + "=" + c_value;
        }

        function getCookie(c_name) {
            var i, x, y, ARRcookies = document.cookie.split(";");
            for (i = 0; i < ARRcookies.length; i++) {
                x = ARRcookies[i].substr(0, ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
                y = ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=") + 1);
                x = x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, "");
                if (x == c_name) {
                    return unescape(y);
                }
            }
        }

        try {
            var currentUrl = window.location.pathname;
            if (currentUrl == "/" || currentUrl == "/home/") {
                var widgetCookie = getCookie("FairmontWidget");
                if (widgetCookie != null && widgetCookie != '') {
                    var values = widgetCookie.split("|");
                    var countryIndexValue = values[0];
                    var destinationIndexValue = values[1];
                    var propertyIndexValue = values[2];
                    var rateTypeIndexValue = values[3];
                    var promoCodeValue = values[4];
                    var iataCodeValue = values[5];
                    var arrivalValue = values[6];
                    var departureValue = values[7];
                    var roomsValue = values[8];


                    var ddlDestinationClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlDestination';
                    var ddlCityClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlCity';
                    var ddlPropertyClientId = 'ctl00_CphContent_BookingWidget_ddlProperty';

                    var txtArrivalDateClientId = 'txtArrivalDate';
                    var txtDepartureDateClientId = 'txtDepartureDate';

                    if (countryIndexValue != "" && countryIndexValue != undefined)
                        document.getElementById(ddlDestinationClientId).value = countryIndexValue;
                    if (destinationIndexValue != "" && destinationIndexValue != undefined)
                        document.getElementById(ddlCityClientId).value = destinationIndexValue;
                    if (propertyIndexValue != "" && propertyIndexValue != undefined)
                        document.getElementById(ddlPropertyClientId).value = propertyIndexValue;

                    if (arrivalValue != "" && arrivalValue != undefined)
                        document.getElementById(txtArrivalDateClientId).value = arrivalValue;
                    if (departureValue != "" && departureValue != undefined)
                        document.getElementById(txtDepartureDateClientId).value = departureValue;

                }
            }
        }
        catch (ex) {
        }
       </script>
      </div>
     </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
            showMoreLessModule.bindEvents('250');
            stickyHeaderActivityDetails.bindEvents();
            brandHomePageBanner.init();
            BookingWidget.init();
            propertyFilter.init();
            $(window).resize();

            $("button.play-pause-btn").on('click', function () {
                var _self = $(this).find('.play-pause-anime');
                if ($('#proposalSliderNav').get(0).slick.options.autoplay) {
                    $("#proposalSliderNav").slick("slickSetOption", "autoplay", false, true);
                    $(_self).removeClass('pause').addClass('play');
                    $(this).find(".text-change").text("Play Slider");
                }
                else {
                    $("#proposalSliderNav").slick("slickSetOption", "autoplay", true, true);
                    $(_self).removeClass('play').addClass('pause');
                    $(this).find(".text-change").text("Pause Slider");
                }

            });

            $(window).load(function () {
                $("[id$=ddlProperty]").trigger("change");
                $("[id$=ddlProperty]").blur();
                $(".skip-link").focus();
                $(".skip-link").blur();
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $(".processing-popup-container .img-holder img").attr("src", $(".processing-popup-container .img-holder img").data("src"));
                    $("#proposalSliderNav").slick("slickSetOption", "autoplay", true, true);
                    $('#proposalSlider').slick("slickSetOption", "infinite", true, true);
                }, 3000);
            })
        });
   </script>
